<p><b>Steven George Gerrard</b>, <span style="font-size:85%;"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Member_of_the_Order_of_the_British_Empire" title="Member of the Order of the British Empire">MBE</a></span> (born 30 May 1980) is a English former professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who played as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>. He spent the majority of his career playing for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>, with most of that time as their <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a>. He will become the full-time coach of <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C._Reserves_and_Academy" title="Liverpool F.C. Reserves and Academy">Liverpool Academy</a> in February 2017<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<p>Gerrard spent 17 seasons at <a href="/wiki/Anfield" title="Anfield">Anfield</a>, making his Liverpool debut in 1998, cementing his place in the first team in 2000, and succeeding <a href="/wiki/Sami_Hyypi%C3%A4" title="Sami Hyypiä">Sami Hyypiä</a> as team captain in 2003. His honours include two <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cups</a>, three <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Football_League_Cup" title="Football League Cup">League Cups</a>, one <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>, one <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Cup</a>, and one <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Super_Cup" title="UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a>. Gerrard scored Liverpool's first goal and won the penalty kick for the third as Liverpool came from 3–0 down to defeat <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2005_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2005 UEFA Champions League Final">2005 Champions League Final</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> He joined <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a> club <a href="/wiki/LA_Galaxy" title="LA Galaxy">LA Galaxy</a> in July 2015,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> spending one-and-a-half seasons there before retiring on 24 November 2016.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></p>
<p>Gerrard made his international debut for the <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England national football team</a> in 2000, and represented his country at the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2000" title="UEFA Euro 2000">2000</a>, <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2004" title="UEFA Euro 2004">2004</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">2012</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Football_Championship" title="UEFA European Football Championship">UEFA European Football Championships</a>, as well as the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006</a>, <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010</a> and <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014</a> <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cups</a> – captaining the team at the latter two tournaments.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-8">[8]</a></sup> He was named as the permanent England captain shortly before UEFA Euro 2012,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> where he was named in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012#Awards" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Team of the Tournament</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup> Gerrard became the sixth player to win <a href="/wiki/List_of_footballers_with_100_or_more_caps" title="List of footballers with 100 or more caps">100 caps</a> for England in 2012,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11"><a href="#cite_note-11">[11]</a></sup> and is currently third in the country's <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team#Most_capped_players" title="England national football team">all-time appearance list</a>. He ended his international career in July 2014, having won 114 caps.</p>
<p>Regarded to be one of the greatest midfielders of his generation,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[12]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ronaldinho_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-Ronaldinho-14">[14]</a></sup> Gerrard came second to <a href="/wiki/Kenny_Dalglish" title="Kenny Dalglish">Kenny Dalglish</a> in the "100 Players Who Shook The Kop", a 2008 Liverpool fan poll, and first in 2013.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15"><a href="#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[16]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pel%C3%A9" title="Pelé">Pelé</a> said in 2009 that they considered Gerrard to be the best footballer in the world.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> In 2005, Gerrard was honoured as the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Club_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Club Footballer of the Year">UEFA Club Footballer of the Year</a> and won the <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d'Or">Ballon d'Or Bronze Award</a>. He has also been named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="PFA Team of the Year">PFA Team of the Year</a> a record eight times, the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FIFPro_World_XI" title="FIFPro World XI">FIFA World XI</a> three times, and was named <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players' Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a> in 2006 and the <a href="/wiki/FWA_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="FWA Footballer of the Year">FWA Footballer of the Year</a> in 2009. He is, to date, the only footballer ever to have scored a goal in an <a href="/wiki/2006_FA_Cup_Final" title="2006 FA Cup Final">FA Cup Final</a>, a <a href="/wiki/2003_Football_League_Cup_Final" title="2003 Football League Cup Final">League Cup Final</a>, a <a href="/wiki/2001_UEFA_Cup_Final" title="2001 UEFA Cup Final">UEFA Cup Final</a> and a <a href="/wiki/2005_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2005 UEFA Champions League Final">UEFA Champions League Final</a>, also being on the winning team on each occasion.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Record_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-Record-19">[19]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>
